The hotel environment is very good, full of green, the air is great, and it is very quiet. It is very comfortable to take a walk after dinner.
The hotel is only a 14-minute walk from Zhaisha Dong Village, and it is also very convenient to walk there for a meal.
The hotel provides a pick-up service for Fanjing Mountain. When you check in, you can make an appoin**ent for the departure time the next day. If you call the hotel when you go down the mountain, you will pick it up.
In addition, if you are not driving by yourself, the passenger transport center is opposite the high-speed rail at Tongren Station. You can tell the driver that the bus will drop you off when it passes by the hotel; there are also buses from Fanjing Mountain Scenic Area that go directly to Tongren Station, which is super convenient!
